Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

==PAGE:152==
Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Acrimo VS 1382 Screen, 
one year.prd
Page

==PAGE:171==
Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.

==PAGE:263==
Notes:
One of the product types in Acrimo's product portfolio is the VS 1382 Screen, which is one out of four exterior and wind tolerant 
screen models that Acrimo offers. Just as other of Acrimos products, the VS 1382 Screen is offered in various sizes. The VS 1382 
Screen is considered to consist of three assembled units: a Screen case, a Motor unit and a ZIP-control. Each assembly unit  
consist of multiple components, constructed from various kind of materials and suppliers. The intended study means to use a VS
1382 Screen as case product in the assessment. In 2019, Acrimo sold a total amount of 166 VS 1382 screens and the average 
measurements on all of them is 2910mmx2290mmx116mm, and is therefor the size the assessment means to use to calculate the 
products environmental impact.
